// GlobalUsings.cs вҖ“ ГЎp dб»Ҙng cho toГ n bб»ҷ Application project
//
// вҡ  LЖҜU Гқ QUAN TRб»ҢNG:
//   "global using Alias = Type" KHГ”NG hб»— trб»Ј type-arguments (e.g. Alias<T>)
//   вҶ’ KHГ”NG dГ№ng kiб»ғu Д‘Гі. Chб»ү import namespace bГ¬nh thЖ°б»қng nhЖ° bГӘn dЖ°б»ӣi.
//
// Nhб»қ dГІng nГ y, mб»Қi file trong project Д‘б»Ғu dГ№ng Д‘Ж°б»Јc Task<T>
// dГ№ namespace cб»§a file lГ  Services.Tasks (dб»… gГўy nhбә§m vб»ӣi C# Task).
global using System.Threading.Tasks;


========================================
--- FILE: WorkflowConstants.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Constants
{
    public static class WorkflowConstants
    {
        public static string GetStatusName(int id) => id switch
        {
            1 => "CREATED",
            2 => "ASSIGNED",
            3 => "IN-PROGRESS",
            4 => "FAILED",
            5 => "REVIEW-1",
            6 => "REVIEW-2",
            7 => "APPROVED",
            8 => "IN-TEST",
            9 => "RESOLVED",
            10 => "CLOSED",
            _ => $"STATUS-{id}"
        };

        public static string GetPriorityName(int id) => id switch
        {
            4 => "Critical",
            3 => "High",
            2 => "Medium",
            1 => "Low",
            _ => "Unknown"
        };
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: AuthDTOs.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs
{
    // =====================================================
    // DTO (Data Transfer Object) вҖ“ Д‘б»‘i tЖ°б»Јng truyб»Ғn dб»Ҝ liб»Үu giб»Ҝa cГЎc tбә§ng
    //
    // TбәЎi sao cбә§n DTO thay vГ¬ truyб»Ғn Entity thбәіng?
    //   Entity chб»©a tбәҘt cбәЈ cб»ҷt DB (kб»ғ cбәЈ PasswordHash, CreatedAt...)
    //   DTO chб»ү chб»©a Д‘Гәng dб»Ҝ liб»Үu tбә§ng trГӘn cбә§n biбәҝt
    //   вҶ’ an toГ n hЖЎn, giбәЈm coupling giб»Ҝa tбә§ng
    // =====================================================

    /// <summary>
    /// Kбәҝt quбәЈ trбәЈ vб»Ғ sau khi gб»Қi IAuthService.LoginAsync().
    ///
    /// DГ№ng Result Pattern thay vГ¬ throw Exception cho lб»—i nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ:
    ///   - Form dб»… kiб»ғm tra: if (!result.Success) { lblError.Text = result.ErrorMessage; }
    ///   - KhГҙng cбә§n try-catch cho lб»—i "sai mбәӯt khбә©u" (Д‘Гўy khГҙng phбәЈi exception)
    ///   - Exception chб»ү dГ nh cho lб»—i hбәЎ tбә§ng (DB mбәҘt kбәҝt nб»‘i, ...)
    /// </summary>
    public class LoginResult
    {
        public bool   Success      { get; init; }
        public string? ErrorMessage { get; init; } // null khi thГ nh cГҙng
        public UserSessionDto? User { get; init; } // null khi thбәҘt bбәЎi

        // Factory methods вҖ“ tбәЎo kбәҝt quбәЈ rГө nghД©a, khГҙng new trб»ұc tiбәҝp
        public static LoginResult Ok(UserSessionDto user)
            => new() { Success = true, User = user };

        public static LoginResult Fail(string message)
            => new() { Success = false, ErrorMessage = message };
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// ThГҙng tin user cбә§n thiбәҝt sau khi Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp вҖ“ lЖ°u vГ o AppSession.
    ///
    /// Chб»§ Д‘б»ҷng KHГ”NG cГі PasswordHash Д‘б»ғ:
    ///   - KhГҙng vГҙ tГ¬nh lб»ҷ hash ra Form/UI
    ///   - GiбәЈm dб»Ҝ liб»Үu khГҙng cбә§n thiбәҝt trong bб»ҷ nhб»ӣ
    /// </summary>
    public class UserSessionDto
    {
        public int    Id         { get; init; }
        public string Username   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string FullName   { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string Email      { get; init; } = string.Empty;
        public string? AvatarPath { get; init; }

        // Danh sГЎch tГӘn role: ["Admin"], ["Manager"], ["Developer"]
        // DГ№ng Д‘б»ғ kiб»ғm tra quyб»Ғn trong AppSession (IsAdmin, IsManager...)
        public List<string> Roles { get; init; } = new();
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: DashboardDTOs.cs ---
========================================

using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs
{
    // =====================================================
    // DTO cho GДҗ6: Dashboard & Thб»‘ng kГӘ
    // Cung cбәҘp sб»‘ liб»Үu tб»•ng quan cho mГ n hГ¬nh Admin/Manager
    // =====================================================

    public class DashboardStatsDto
    {
        public int TotalTasks { get; set; }
        public int CompletedTasks { get; set; }
        public int OverdueTasks { get; set; }
        public int DueSoonTasks { get; set; }
        public List<StatusSummaryDto> StatusSummaries { get; set; } = new List<StatusSummaryDto>();
        public List<ProjectProgressDto> ProjectProgresses { get; set; } = new List<ProjectProgressDto>();
    }

    public class StatusSummaryDto
    {
        public string StatusName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public int Count { get; set; }
        public string ColorHex { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    public class ProjectProgressDto
    {
        public string ProjectName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        // ДҗГғ FIX: Дҗб»•i sang decimal Д‘б»ғ Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ Д‘б»ҷ chГӯnh xГЎc vб»ӣi Budget
        public decimal ProgressPercentage { get; set; }
    }

    public class BudgetReportDto
    {
        public string ProjectName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public decimal Budget { get; set; }
        public decimal TotalExpense { get; set; }
        public decimal Remaining => Budget - TotalExpense;
        public decimal UsagePercentage => Budget > 0 ? Math.Round((TotalExpense / Budget) * 100m, 1) : 0m;
    }

    public class ProgressReportDto
    {
        public string ProjectName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public int TotalTasks { get; set; }
        public int CompletedTasks { get; set; }
        public decimal AvgProgress { get; set; }
        public string Status { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    }

    public class ProjectBudgetSummaryDto
    {
        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public string ProjectName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
        public decimal Budget { get; set; }
        public decimal TotalExpense { get; set; }
        public decimal Remaining => Budget - TotalExpense;

        public decimal UsagePercent => Budget > 0
            ? Math.Round((TotalExpense / Budget) * 100m, 1)
            : 0m;

        public bool IsOverBudget => TotalExpense > Budget && Budget > 0;
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: ExpenseReportDto.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs
{
    /// <summary>
    /// DTO chuyГӘn biб»Үt cho bГЎo cГЎo Chi phГӯ &amp; NgГўn sГЎch (Giai Д‘oбәЎn 9 вҖ“ UC-Report-01).
    ///
    /// Thiбәҝt kбәҝ "Flat DTO":
    ///   - Kбәҝt hб»Јp dб»Ҝ liб»Үu tб»« Project, Customer, Owner (Manager) vГ  SUM(Expense.Amount)
    ///     thГ nh mб»ҷt Д‘б»‘i tЖ°б»Јng phбәіng, khГҙng cГі navigation property.
    ///   - ДҗЖ°б»Јc tбәЎo trб»ұc tiбәҝp bбәұng Projection (.Select()) trong ExpenseRepository
    ///     вҶ’ TrГЎnh nбәЎp toГ n bб»ҷ Entity vГ o bб»ҷ nhб»ӣ (N+1, eager-loading thб»«a).
    ///
    /// Constraint VГ ng: TбәҘt cбәЈ trЖ°б»қng tiб»Ғn tб»Ү PHбәўI dГ№ng decimal (KHГ”NG dГ№ng double/float).
    /// </summary>
    public class ExpenseReportDto
    {
        // в”Җв”Җ ThГҙng tin Dб»ұ ГЎn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>ID dб»ұ ГЎn вҖ“ dГ№ng Д‘б»ғ group hoбә·c filter б»ҹ tбә§ng Service.</summary>
        public int ProjectId { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TГӘn dб»ұ ГЎn.</summary>
        public string ProjectName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>TrбәЎng thГЎi dб»ұ ГЎn: NotStarted | InProgress | OnHold | Completed | Cancelled.</summary>
        public string ProjectStatus { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        // в”Җв”Җ ThГҙng tin KhГЎch hГ ng в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>TГӘn khГЎch hГ ng. TrбәЈ vб»Ғ "вҖ”" nбәҝu dб»ұ ГЎn chЖ°a gГЎn khГЎch hГ ng.</summary>
        public string CustomerName { get; set; } = "вҖ”";

        // в”Җв”Җ ThГҙng tin QuбәЈn lГҪ dб»ұ ГЎn (Owner) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Hб»Қ tГӘn Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ cб»§a ngЖ°б»қi quбәЈn lГҪ dб»ұ ГЎn (Project.Owner.FullName).</summary>
        public string ManagerName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        // в”Җв”Җ TГ i chГӯnh (decimal вҖ“ Constraint VГ ng) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>NgГўn sГЎch ban Д‘бә§u cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn (Project.Budget). Kiб»ғu decimal(18,2).</summary>
        public decimal Budget { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Tб»•ng chi phГӯ thб»ұc tбәҝ = SUM(Expense.Amount) cб»§a tбәҘt cбәЈ chi phГӯ thuб»ҷc dб»ұ ГЎn.
        /// Kiб»ғu decimal вҖ“ tб»•ng hб»Јp tбәЎi tбә§ng Database qua GroupBy + Sum.
        /// </summary>
        public decimal TotalExpense { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Sб»‘ tiб»Ғn cГІn lбәЎi = Budget вҖ“ TotalExpense. TГӯnh tбәЎi computed property.</summary>
        public decimal Remaining => Budget - TotalExpense;

        /// <summary>
        /// Tб»· lб»Ү sб»ӯ dб»Ҙng ngГўn sГЎch (%) = TotalExpense / Budget * 100.
        /// LГ m trГІn 1 chб»Ҝ sб»‘ thбәӯp phГўn. TrбәЈ vб»Ғ 0 nбәҝu Budget = 0 (trГЎnh chia zero).
        /// Kiб»ғu decimal вҖ“ KHГ”NG dГ№ng double.
        /// </summary>
        public decimal UsagePercent => Budget > 0
            ? Math.Round((TotalExpense / Budget) * 100m, 1)
            : 0m;

        /// <summary>Cб»қ cбәЈnh bГЎo: TotalExpense vЖ°б»Јt quГЎ Budget.</summary>
        public bool IsOverBudget => TotalExpense > Budget && Budget > 0;

        // в”Җв”Җ Metadata thб»қi gian в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>NgГ y bбәҜt Д‘бә§u dб»ұ ГЎn.</summary>
        public DateTime StartDate { get; set; }

        /// <summary>NgГ y kбәҝt thГәc dб»ұ kiбәҝn cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn.</summary>
        public DateTime? PlannedEndDate { get; set; }
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    public class Attachment
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        [Required, MaxLength(255)]
        public string FileName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [Required, MaxLength(500)]
        public string FilePath { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(100)]
        public string? ContentType { get; set; }

        public long FileSizeBytes { get; set; }

        public DateTime UploadedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public int TaskItemId { get; set; }
        public TaskItem TaskItem { get; set; } = null!;

        public int UploadedById { get; set; }
        public User UploadedBy { get; set; } = null!;
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// KhГЎch hГ ng - Д‘ЖЎn vб»Ӣ yГӘu cбә§u phГЎt triб»ғn dб»ұ ГЎn
    /// </summary>
    public class Customer
    {

        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string CompanyName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.Schema;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Chi phГӯ phГЎt sinh trong dб»ұ ГЎn
    /// </summary>
    public class Expense
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public Project Project { get; set; } = null!;

        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string ExpenseType { get; set; } = string.Empty; // NhГўn cГҙng / Phбә§n mб»Ғm / HбәЎ tбә§ng

        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(18,2)")]
        public decimal Amount { get; set; }

        public DateOnly ExpenseDate { get; set; }

        [MaxLength(300)]
        public string? Note { get; set; }

        public int CreatedById { get; set; }
        public User CreatedBy { get; set; } = null!;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
    }
}

========================================
--- FILE: Project.cs ---
========================================

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.Schema;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    public class Project
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        // ---- KhГЎch hГ ng ----
        public int? CustomerId { get; set; }
        public Customer? Customer { get; set; }

        // ---- NgЖ°б»қi sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu / PM ----
        public int OwnerId { get; set; }
        public User Owner { get; set; } = null!;

        // ---- Timeline ----
        public DateOnly StartDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? PlannedEndDate { get; set; }
        public DateOnly? ActualEndDate { get; set; }

        // ---- NgГўn sГЎch ----
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(18,2)")]
        public decimal Budget { get; set; } = 0;

        // ---- TrбәЎng thГЎi & ЖҜu tiГӘn ----
        /// <summary>NotStarted | InProgress | OnHold | Completed | Cancelled</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(30)]
        public string Status { get; set; } = "NotStarted";

        /// <summary>1=Low | 2=Medium | 3=High | 4=Critical</summary>
        public byte Priority { get; set; } = 2;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();
        public ICollection<ProjectMember> Members { get; set; } = new List<ProjectMember>();
        public ICollection<Expense> Expenses { get; set; } = new List<Expense>();

        /* ================= COMPUTED (khГҙng map DB) ================= */
        [NotMapped]
        public decimal TotalExpense => Expenses?.Sum(e => e.Amount) ?? 0;

        [NotMapped]
        public int ProgressPercent
        {
            get
            {
                var rootTasks = Tasks?.Where(t => t.ParentTaskId == null).ToList();
                if (rootTasks == null || rootTasks.Count == 0) return 0;
                return (int)rootTasks.Average(t => t.ProgressPercent);
            }
        }
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// BбәЈng trung gian: ThГ nh viГӘn tham gia dб»ұ ГЎn + vai trГІ trong dб»ұ ГЎn
    /// </summary>
    public class ProjectMember
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public Project Project { get; set; } = null!;

        public int UserId { get; set; }
        public User User { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>Developer | Tester | BA | Tech Lead | PM</summary>
        [MaxLength(50)]
        public string? ProjectRole { get; set; }

        public DateTime JoinedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        public DateTime? LeftAt { get; set; }
    }
}

========================================
--- FILE: Status.cs ---
========================================

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// TrбәЎng thГЎi cГҙng viб»Үc вҖ” workflow 10 bЖ°б»ӣc quбәЈn lГҪ dб»ұ ГЎn phбә§n mб»Ғm.
    /// 
    /// Luб»“ng chГӯnh:
    ///   CREATED вҶ’ ASSIGNED вҶ’ IN-PROGRESS вҶ’ REVIEW-1 вҶ’ REVIEW-2 вҶ’ APPROVED вҶ’ IN-TEST вҶ’ RESOLVED вҶ’ CLOSED
    /// Luб»“ng reject:
    ///   REVIEW-1 / REVIEW-2 / IN-TEST вҶ’ FAILED вҶ’ IN-PROGRESS (sб»ӯa lбәЎi)
    /// </summary>
    public class Status
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TГӘn trбәЎng thГЎi (VD: CREATED, IN-PROGRESS, REVIEW-1...).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(50)]
        public string Name { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>MГҙ tбәЈ cГҙng dб»Ҙng cб»§a trбәЎng thГЎi (hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ trГӘn UI).</summary>
        [MaxLength(300)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        public byte DisplayOrder { get; set; } = 0;

        /// <summary>MГЈ mГ u hex Д‘б»ғ tГҙ mГ u trГӘn giao diб»Үn (VD: #4CAF50).</summary>
        [MaxLength(7)]
        public string? ColorHex { get; set; }

        public ICollection<TaskItem> TaskItems { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

--- FILE: TaskItem.cs ---

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations.Schema;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// CГҙng viб»Үc (Task) trong dб»ұ ГЎn.
    /// 
    /// Workflow 10 trбәЎng thГЎi:
    ///   CREATED вҶ’ ASSIGNED вҶ’ IN-PROGRESS вҶ’ REVIEW-1 вҶ’ REVIEW-2 вҶ’ APPROVED вҶ’ IN-TEST вҶ’ RESOLVED вҶ’ CLOSED
    ///                             вҶ‘             вҶ“          вҶ“                     вҶ“
    ///                             в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ FAILED вҶҗв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳвҶҗв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
    /// 
    /// Mб»—i giai Д‘oбәЎn cГі ngЖ°б»қi phб»Ҙ trГЎch riГӘng:
    ///   - AssignedTo: ngЖ°б»қi lГ m task (Developer)
    ///   - Reviewer1: ngЖ°б»қi review lбә§n 1 (peer/team lead)
    ///   - Reviewer2: ngЖ°б»қi review lбә§n 2 (senior/architect)
    ///   - Tester: ngЖ°б»қi kiб»ғm thб»ӯ (QA)
    /// 
    /// Luб»“ng gГЎn ngЖ°б»қi:
    ///   TбәЎo task вҶ’ gГЎn Assignee
    ///   Assignee xong вҶ’ chuyб»ғn REVIEW-1 + gГЎn Reviewer1
    ///   Reviewer1 pass вҶ’ chuyб»ғn REVIEW-2 + gГЎn Reviewer2
    ///   Reviewer2 pass вҶ’ APPROVED вҶ’ IN-TEST + gГЎn Tester
    ///   BбәҘt kб»і ai (Reviewer1/2, Tester) reject вҶ’ FAILED вҶ’ Assignee sб»ӯa lбәЎi
    /// </summary>
    public class TaskItem
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TiГӘu Д‘б»Ғ cГҙng viб»Үc (bбәҜt buб»ҷc, tб»‘i Д‘a 200 kГҪ tб»ұ).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(200)]
        public string Title { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>MГҙ tбәЈ chi tiбәҝt cГҙng viб»Үc (tГ№y chб»Қn, tб»‘i Д‘a 2000 kГҪ tб»ұ).</summary>
        [MaxLength(2000)]
        public string? Description { get; set; }

        /// <summary>ДҗГЎnh dбәҘu task Д‘ГЈ hoГ n thГ nh (tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng set khi ProgressPercent = 100).</summary>
        public bool IsCompleted { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Phбә§n trДғm hoГ n thГ nh: 0вҖ“100. Khi = 100 вҶ’ IsCompleted = true.</summary>
        [Range(0, 100)]
        public byte ProgressPercent { get; set; } = 0;

        /// <summary>Sб»‘ giб»қ Ж°б»ӣc tГӯnh Д‘б»ғ hoГ n thГ nh task.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? EstimatedHours { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Sб»‘ giб»қ thб»ұc tбәҝ Д‘ГЈ lГ m.</summary>
        [Column(TypeName = "decimal(6,1)")]
        public decimal? ActualHours { get; set; }

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime UpdatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;

        /// <summary>HбәЎn chГіt hoГ n thГ nh task.</summary>
        public DateTime? DueDate { get; set; }

        /// <summary>Thб»қi Д‘iб»ғm task Д‘Ж°б»Јc Д‘ГЎnh dбәҘu hoГ n thГ nh (status = RESOLVED/CLOSED).</summary>
        public DateTime? CompletedAt { get; set; }

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */

        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn chб»©a task nГ y.</summary>
        public int ProjectId { get; set; }
        public Project Project { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>Task cha (hб»— trб»Ј sub-task lб»“ng nhau, null = task gб»‘c).</summary>
        public int? ParentTaskId { get; set; }
        public TaskItem? ParentTask { get; set; }
        public ICollection<TaskItem> SubTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>NgЖ°б»қi tбәЎo task.</summary>
        public int CreatedById { get; set; }
        public User CreatedBy { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>NgЖ°б»қi Д‘Ж°б»Јc giao thб»ұc hiб»Үn task (Developer chГӯnh).</summary>
        public int? AssignedToId { get; set; }
        public User? AssignedTo { get; set; }

        // в”Җв”Җ GD3: Workflow Review & Test в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// NgЖ°б»қi review lбә§n 1 (peer review / team lead).
        /// ДҗЖ°б»Јc gГЎn khi Assignee chuyб»ғn task sang REVIEW-1.
        /// </summary>
        public int? Reviewer1Id { get; set; }
        public User? Reviewer1 { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// NgЖ°б»қi review lбә§n 2 (senior developer / architect).
        /// ДҗЖ°б»Јc gГЎn khi Reviewer1 approve vГ  chuyб»ғn sang REVIEW-2.
        /// </summary>
        public int? Reviewer2Id { get; set; }
        public User? Reviewer2 { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// NgЖ°б»қi kiб»ғm thб»ӯ (QA / Tester).
        /// ДҗЖ°б»Јc gГЎn khi Reviewer2 approve vГ  chuyб»ғn sang IN-TEST.
        /// </summary>
        public int? TesterId { get; set; }
        public User? Tester { get; set; }

        // в”Җв”Җ Lookup tables в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Mб»©c Д‘б»ҷ Ж°u tiГӘn (Low / Medium / High / Critical).</summary>
        public int PriorityId { get; set; }
        public Priority Priority { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>TrбәЎng thГЎi hiб»Үn tбәЎi trong workflow 10 bЖ°б»ӣc.</summary>
        public int StatusId { get; set; }
        public Status Status { get; set; } = null!;

        /// <summary>PhГўn loбәЎi task (Bug / Feature / Improvement / Research / Testing).</summary>
        public int CategoryId { get; set; }
        public Category Category { get; set; } = null!;

        // в”Җв”Җ Collections в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch bГ¬nh luбәӯn trГӘn task.</summary>
        public ICollection<Comment> Comments { get; set; } = new List<Comment>();

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch file Д‘Гӯnh kГЁm.</summary>
        public ICollection<Attachment> Attachments { get; set; } = new List<Attachment>();

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch tag gбәҜn trГӘn task.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskTag> TaskTags { get; set; } = new List<TaskTag>();
    }
}

using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities
{
    /// <summary>
    /// TГ i khoбәЈn ngЖ°б»қi dГ№ng trong hб»Ү thб»‘ng.
    /// Mб»ҷt user cГі thб»ғ Д‘Гіng nhiб»Ғu vai trГІ trГӘn task: Assignee, Reviewer, Tester.
    /// </summary>
    public class User
    {
        public int Id { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TГӘn Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp (unique, dГ№ng lГ m khГіa nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(50)]
        public string Username { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Hб»Қ vГ  tГӘn Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§.</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string FullName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Email (unique).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(100)]
        public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        /// <summary>Mбәӯt khбә©u Д‘ГЈ hash bбәұng BCrypt (WorkFactor 12).</summary>
        [Required, MaxLength(256)]
        public string PasswordHash { get; set; } = string.Empty;

        [MaxLength(20)]
        public string? Phone { get; set; }

        [MaxLength(255)]
        public string? AvatarPath { get; set; }

        /// <summary>TГ i khoбәЈn active hay bб»Ӣ vГҙ hiб»Үu hГіa (soft delete).</summary>
        public bool IsActive { get; set; } = true;

        public DateTime CreatedAt { get; set; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
        public DateTime? LastLogin { get; set; }

        /* ================= RELATIONSHIPS ================= */

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch role cб»§a user (Admin / Manager / Developer).</summary>
        public ICollection<UserRole> UserRoles { get; set; } = new List<UserRole>();

        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn user lГ m Owner/PM.</summary>
        public ICollection<Project> OwnedProjects { get; set; } = new List<Project>();

        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn user tham gia (qua bбәЈng ProjectMembers).</summary>
        public ICollection<ProjectMember> ProjectMemberships { get; set; } = new List<ProjectMember>();

        /// <summary>Task do user tбәЎo.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> CreatedTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task Д‘Ж°б»Јc giao cho user thб»ұc hiб»Үn.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> AssignedTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        // в”Җв”Җ GD3: Workflow Review & Test в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Task user lГ m Reviewer lбә§n 1.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Review1Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task user lГ m Reviewer lбә§n 2.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> Review2Tasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>Task user lГ m Tester.</summary>
        public ICollection<TaskItem> TesterTasks { get; set; } = new List<TaskItem>();

        /// <summary>BГ¬nh luбәӯn cб»§a user.</summary>
        public ICollection<Comment> Comments { get; set; } = new List<Comment>();

        /// <summary>Chi phГӯ do user tбәЎo.</summary>
        public ICollection<Expense> CreatedExpenses { get; set; } = new List<Expense>();
    }
}

========================================
--- FILE: PasswordHelper.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Tбәӯp trung logic hash/verify mбәӯt khбә©u bбәұng BCrypt.
    ///
    /// TбәЎi sao BCrypt thay vГ¬ SHA-256?
    ///   SHA-256: thuбәӯt toГЎn hash nhanh, GPU cГі thб»ғ thб»ӯ 10 tб»· hash/giГўy вҶ’ dб»… brute-force
    ///   BCrypt:  cб»‘ tГ¬nh chбәӯm (~300ms/hash), cГі cost factor Д‘iб»Ғu chб»үnh Д‘Ж°б»Јc
    ///            tб»ұ sinh salt ngбә«u nhiГӘn cho mб»—i password вҶ’ chб»‘ng rainbow table
    ///
    /// TбәЎi sao tГЎch ra Helper riГӘng?
    ///   AuthService vГ  UserService Д‘б»Ғu cбә§n hash/verify
    ///   вҶ’ Д‘бә·t 1 chб»— trГЎnh duplicate code, dб»… Д‘б»•i thuбәӯt toГЎn sau nГ y
    /// </summary>
    public static class PasswordHelper
    {
        // WorkFactor 12 = 2^12 = 4096 vГІng lбә·p nб»ҷi bб»ҷ вҶ’ ~300ms trГӘn CPU thГҙng thЖ°б»қng
        // TДғng lГӘn 13-14 nбәҝu server mбәЎnh hЖЎn (mб»—i +1 tДғng gбәҘp Д‘Гҙi thб»қi gian hash)
        private const int WorkFactor = 12;

        /// <summary>
        /// Hash mбәӯt khбә©u bбәұng BCrypt. Salt ngбә«u nhiГӘn Д‘Ж°б»Јc tбәЎo tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng,
        /// nhГәng vГ o trong chuб»—i hash вҶ’ khГҙng cбә§n lЖ°u salt riГӘng.
        /// </summary>
        public static string Hash(string plainPassword)
            => BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.HashPassword(plainPassword, WorkFactor);

        /// <summary>
        /// XГЎc minh mбәӯt khбә©u nhбәӯp vГ o vб»ӣi hash Д‘ГЈ lЖ°u trong DB.
        /// BCrypt tб»ұ extract salt tб»« hash вҶ’ truyб»Ғn vГ o Д‘Гәng 2 tham sб»‘ lГ  Д‘б»§.
        /// </summary>
        public static bool Verify(string plainPassword, string hashedPassword)
        {
            try
            {
                return BCrypt.Net.BCrypt.Verify(plainPassword, hashedPassword);
            }
            catch
            {
                // BбәҜt trЖ°б»қng hб»Јp hash format cЕ© (SHA-256) vбә«n cГІn trong DB
                // вҶ’ trбәЈ false thay vГ¬ crash app
                return false;
            }
        }
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: ValidationHelper.cs ---
========================================

using System.Net.Mail;
using System.Text.RegularExpressions;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Tбәӯp trung toГ n bб»ҷ quy tбәҜc validate dГ№ng chung cho cГЎc Service.
    /// Дҗбә·t 1 chб»— Д‘б»ғ khi thay Д‘б»•i quy tбәҜc chб»ү sб»ӯa б»ҹ Д‘Гўy, ГЎp dб»Ҙng toГ n app.
    /// </summary>
    public static class ValidationHelper
    {
        /// <summary>Mбәӯt khбә©u hб»Јp lб»Ү: tб»‘i thiб»ғu 6 kГҪ tб»ұ, khГҙng chб»ү khoбәЈng trбәҜng.</summary>
        public static bool IsPasswordStrong(string password)
            => !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password) && password.Length >= 6;

        /// <summary>Email hб»Јp lб»Ү theo chuбә©n RFC (dГ№ng MailAddress Д‘б»ғ parse).</summary>
        public static bool IsValidEmail(string email)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(email)) return false;
            try
            {
                var addr = new MailAddress(email);
                return addr.Address == email.Trim();
            }
            catch { return false; }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Username hб»Јp lб»Ү: 3-50 kГҪ tб»ұ, chб»ү chб»Ҝ cГЎi, sб»‘ vГ  dбәҘu gбәЎch dЖ°б»ӣi.
        /// Regex: ^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$
        /// </summary>
        public static bool IsValidUsername(string username)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username)) return false;
            return Regex.IsMatch(username, @"^[a-zA-Z0-9_]{3,50}$");
        }
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Repository cho Expense вҖ“ CRUD chi phГӯ dб»ұ ГЎn (GДҗ8: UC-23 / GДҗ9: UC-Report-01).
    /// Kбәҝ thб»«a IRepository&lt;Expense&gt; вҶ’ cГі sбәөn GetByIdAsync, GetAllAsync, AddAsync, UpdateAsync, DeleteAsync.
    /// </summary>
    public interface IExpenseRepository : IRepository<Expense>
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy danh sГЎch chi phГӯ cб»§a mб»ҷt dб»ұ ГЎn, kГЁm thГҙng tin ngЖ°б»қi tбәЎo (CreatedBy).
        /// SбәҜp xбәҝp theo ExpenseDate giбәЈm dбә§n (mб»ӣi nhбәҘt lГӘn Д‘бә§u).
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<Expense>> GetByProjectAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>
        /// TГӯnh tб»•ng chi phГӯ thб»ұc tбәҝ cб»§a mб»ҷt dб»ұ ГЎn trб»ұc tiбәҝp trГӘn DB (SUM aggregation).
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ 0 nбәҝu chЖ°a cГі chi phГӯ nГ o.
        /// Kбәҝt quбәЈ lГ  decimal вҖ“ KHГ”NG dГ№ng double/float.
        /// </summary>
        Task<decimal> GetTotalByProjectAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy dб»Ҝ liб»Үu bГЎo cГЎo chi phГӯ vГ  ngГўn sГЎch dб»ұ ГЎn (GДҗ9: UC-Report-01).
        ///
        /// Kб»№ thuбәӯt quan trб»Қng:
        ///   - DГ№ng .AsNoTracking() вҶ’ chб»ү Д‘б»Қc, khГҙng theo dГөi thay Д‘б»•i Entity.
        ///   - DГ№ng Projection .Select() trб»ұc tiбәҝp sang ExpenseReportDto вҶ’ KHГ”NG nбәЎp Entity thб»«a.
        ///   - GroupJoin (LEFT JOIN) giб»Ҝa Project vГ  Expenses вҶ’ tГӯnh SUM(Amount) trГӘn DB.
        ///   - Bypass quy tбәҜc "chб»ү trбәЈ Entity" вҖ“ Д‘Ж°б»Јc phГ©p cho trЖ°б»қng hб»Јp Report.
        ///
        /// Tham sб»‘:
        ///   - projectId = null вҶ’ tбәҘt cбәЈ dб»ұ ГЎn.
        ///   - projectId cГі giГЎ trб»Ӣ вҶ’ lб»Қc theo dб»ұ ГЎn cб»Ҙ thб»ғ.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<ExpenseReportDto>> GetExpenseReportDataAsync(int? projectId = null);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Repository cho Project вҖ“ CRUD dб»ұ ГЎn + quбәЈn lГҪ thГ nh viГӘn.
    /// </summary>
    public interface IProjectRepository : IRepository<Project>
    {
        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn do user sб»ҹ hб»Ҝu (Owner/PM).</summary>
        Task<List<Project>> GetByOwnerAsync(int ownerId);

        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn mГ  user lГ  thГ nh viГӘn (qua ProjectMembers, LeftAt == null).</summary>
        Task<List<Project>> GetByMemberAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>Chi tiбәҝt dб»ұ ГЎn kГЁm Owner, Customer, Members, Tasks, Expenses.</summary>
        Task<Project?> GetWithDetailsAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>Dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘ang hoбәЎt Д‘б»ҷng (InProgress / NotStarted), sбәҜp theo deadline.</summary>
        Task<List<Project>> GetActiveProjectsAsync();

        /// <summary>Tб»•ng chi phГӯ thб»ұc tбәҝ tб»« bбәЈng Expenses (SUM trГӘn DB).</summary>
        Task<decimal> GetTotalExpenseAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>Cбәӯp nhбәӯt Status + UpdatedAt (ExecuteUpdateAsync, khГҙng load entity).</summary>
        Task UpdateStatusAsync(int projectId, string status);

        // в”Җв”Җ Giai Д‘oбәЎn 3: QuбәЈn lГҪ thГ nh viГӘn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Kiб»ғm tra dб»ұ ГЎn cГі task chЖ°a (dГ№ng trЖ°б»ӣc khi xГіa).</summary>
        Task<bool> HasTasksAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch thГ nh viГӘn Д‘ang active (LeftAt == null) kГЁm thГҙng tin User.</summary>
        Task<List<ProjectMember>> GetMembersAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>ThГӘm thГ nh viГӘn vГ o dб»ұ ГЎn.</summary>
        Task AddMemberAsync(ProjectMember member);

        /// <summary>ДҗГЎnh dбәҘu thГ nh viГӘn rб»қi dб»ұ ГЎn (set LeftAt, khГҙng xГіa thбәӯt).</summary>
        Task RemoveMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId);
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: IRepository.cs ---
========================================

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Generic repository interface вҖ“ tбәҘt cбәЈ repository Д‘б»Ғu kбәҝ thб»«a interface nГ y.
    /// ГҒp dб»Ҙng Repository Pattern: tГЎch biб»Үt logic truy cбәӯp dб»Ҝ liб»Үu khб»Ҹi business logic.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">Kiб»ғu entity (User, Project, TaskItem, ...)</typeparam>
    public interface IRepository<T> where T : class
    {
        /// <summary>LбәҘy 1 bбәЈn ghi theo khГіa chГӯnh. TrбәЈ vб»Ғ null nбәҝu khГҙng tГ¬m thбәҘy.</summary>
        Task<T?> GetByIdAsync(int id);

        /// <summary>LбәҘy toГ n bб»ҷ danh sГЎch. DГ№ng GetPagedAsync nбәҝu dб»Ҝ liб»Үu lб»ӣn.</summary>
        Task<List<T>> GetAllAsync();

        /// <summary>ThГӘm mб»ӣi 1 bбәЈn ghi vГ o database.</summary>
        Task AddAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>Cбәӯp nhбәӯt 1 bбәЈn ghi Д‘ГЈ tб»“n tбәЎi.</summary>
        Task UpdateAsync(T entity);

        /// <summary>XГіa bбәЈn ghi theo ID (hard delete hoбә·c soft delete tГ№y repository).</summary>
        Task DeleteAsync(int id);
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: ITaskRepository.cs ---
========================================

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Task Repository вҖ“ trung tГўm cб»§a hб»Ү thб»‘ng GD4.
    ///
    /// GD4 bб»• sung so vб»ӣi GD1/GD3:
    ///   - GetByIdWithDetailsAsync: eager load Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ cho frmTaskEdit
    ///   - GetByReviewerAsync / GetByTesterAsync: cho mГ n hГ¬nh Review/Test
    ///   - UpdateStatusAsync: chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi workflow 10 bЖ°б»ӣc
    ///   - GetLookupDataAsync: lбәҘy Priority, Status, Category 1 lбә§n cho dropdown
    /// </summary>
    public interface ITaskRepository : IRepository<TaskItem>
    {
        // в”Җв”Җ Truy vбәҘn Д‘ЖЎn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy task kГЁm toГ n bб»ҷ navigation properties.
        /// DГ№ng cho frmTaskEdit (cбә§n hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ Priority, Status, Category, User, SubTasks).
        /// </summary>
        Task<TaskItem?> GetByIdWithDetailsAsync(int taskId);

        // в”Җв”Җ PhГўn trang + lб»Қc Д‘a tiГӘu chГӯ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// PhГўn trang + lб»Қc kбәҝt hб»Јp nhiб»Ғu tiГӘu chГӯ (IQueryable filter chain).
        /// TбәҘt cбәЈ tham sб»‘ nullable = tГ№y chб»Қn, chб»ү WHERE khi cГі giГЎ trб»Ӣ.
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ (Items, TotalCount) Д‘б»ғ tГӯnh sб»‘ trang б»ҹ UI.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(List<TaskItem> Items, int TotalCount)> GetPagedAsync(
            int page,
            int pageSize,
            int?    projectId       = null,
            int?    assignedToId    = null,
            int?    statusId        = null,
            int?    priorityId      = null,
            int?    categoryId      = null,
            string? searchKeyword   = null);

        // в”Җв”Җ Truy vбәҘn theo ngЖ°б»қi phб»Ҙ trГЎch в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Task chЖ°a hoГ n thГ nh Д‘Ж°б»Јc giao cho developer (mГ n hГ¬nh "CГҙng viб»Үc cб»§a tГҙi").
        /// SбәҜp xбәҝp: DueDate tДғng dбә§n (gбә§n deadline lГӘn Д‘бә§u).
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetAssignedToUserAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ review lбә§n 1 bб»ҹi reviewer chб»ү Д‘б»Ӣnh.
        /// Status phбәЈi lГ  REVIEW-1.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByReviewer1Async(int reviewer1Id);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ review lбә§n 2 bб»ҹi reviewer chб»ү Д‘б»Ӣnh.
        /// Status phбәЈi lГ  REVIEW-2.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByReviewer2Async(int reviewer2Id);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ test bб»ҹi tester chб»ү Д‘б»Ӣnh.
        /// Status phбәЈi lГ  IN-TEST.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByTesterAsync(int testerId);

        // в”Җв”Җ Truy vбәҘn theo dб»ұ ГЎn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// TбәҘt cбәЈ task cб»§a 1 dб»ұ ГЎn.
        /// includeSubTasks = false вҶ’ chб»ү lбәҘy task gб»‘c (ParentTaskId == null).
        /// SбәҜp xбәҝp: Priority DESC вҶ’ DueDate ASC.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetByProjectAsync(int projectId, bool includeSubTasks = false);

        // в”Җв”Җ CбәЈnh bГЎo / Dashboard в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Task Д‘ГЈ quГЎ hбәЎn (DueDate &lt; Now vГ  chЖ°a hoГ n thГ nh).</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetOverdueAsync();

        /// <summary>Task sбәҜp Д‘бәҝn hбәЎn trong N ngГ y tб»ӣi (mбә·c Д‘б»Ӣnh 7 ngГ y).</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetDueSoonAsync(int days = 7);

        // в”Җв”Җ Cбәӯp nhбәӯt tб»‘i Ж°u (khГҙng cбә§n load entity) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Cбәӯp nhбәӯt tiбәҝn Д‘б»ҷ % вҖ” tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng set IsCompleted, CompletedAt, vГ  StatusId.
        ///   progress = 100  вҶ’ IsCompleted = true,  CompletedAt = Now, StatusId = RESOLVED
        ///   progress &lt; 100  вҶ’ IsCompleted = false, CompletedAt = null  (mб»ҹ lбәЎi nбәҝu nhбә§m)
        /// DГ№ng ExecuteUpdateAsync вҖ” khГҙng cбә§n SELECT entity trЖ°б»ӣc.
        /// </summary>
        Task UpdateProgressAsync(int taskId, byte progressPercent, int resolvedStatusId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi workflow вҖ” chб»ү update StatusId + UpdatedAt.
        /// DГ№ng ExecuteUpdateAsync вҖ” khГҙng load entity.
        /// </summary>
        Task UpdateStatusAsync(int taskId, int newStatusId);

        /// <summary>
        /// GГЎn ngЖ°б»қi review / tester vГ o task Д‘б»“ng thб»қi chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi.
        /// DГ№ng ExecuteUpdateAsync вҖ” 1 round-trip duy nhбәҘt.
        /// </summary>
        Task AssignReviewerAsync(int taskId, int? reviewer1Id, int? reviewer2Id, int? testerId, int newStatusId);

        // в”Җв”Җ Thб»‘ng kГӘ cho Dashboard в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Дҗбәҝm task theo Status trong 1 dб»ұ ГЎn.
        /// GroupBy trб»ұc tiбәҝp trГӘn DB вҶ’ trбәЈ vб»Ғ Dictionary (Status.Name вҶ’ Count).
        Task<Dictionary<string, int>> GetStatusSummaryByProjectAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Giai Д‘oбәЎn 6: TГӯnh toГЎn sб»‘ lЖ°б»Јng tб»•ng, hoГ n thГ nh, quГЎ hбәЎn, vГ  biб»ғu Д‘б»“ cho Dashboard.
        /// ChбәЎy EF GroupBy Д‘б»ғ tб»‘i Ж°u hiб»Үu nДғng tбәЎi Database.
        /// </summary>
        Task<DashboardStatsDto> GetDashboardStatsAsync(int? projectId = null);

        /// <summary>
        /// Giai Д‘oбәЎn 6: TГӯnh tб»•ng Budget vГ  Actual Expenses theo Project
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<BudgetReportDto>> GetBudgetReportAsync(int? projectId = null);

        /// <summary>
        /// Giai Д‘oбәЎn 6: TГӯnh chi tiбәҝt Task Д‘ГЈ xong vs Tб»•ng sб»‘ Task theo Project
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<ProgressReportDto>> GetProgressReportAsync(int? projectId = null);

        // в”Җв”Җ Lookup data cho dropdown в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Status (10 bЖ°б»ӣc), sбәҜp theo DisplayOrder.</summary>
        Task<List<Status>> GetAllStatusesAsync();

        /// <summary>LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Priority (4 mб»©c), sбәҜp theo Level.</summary>
        Task<List<Priority>> GetAllPrioritiesAsync();

        /// <summary>LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Category (Bug/Feature/...).</summary>
        Task<List<Category>> GetAllCategoriesAsync();

        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetAllByProjectAsync(int projectId);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces
{
    public interface IUserRepository : IRepository<User>
    {
        Task<User?> GetByUsernameAsync(string username);
        Task<User?> GetByEmailAsync(string email);
        Task<User?> GetWithRolesAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>LбәҘy TбәӨT Cбәў user kГЁm Roles (active + inactive) вҖ” dГ№ng cho mГ n hГ¬nh Admin.</summary>
        Task<List<User>> GetAllWithRolesAsync();

        Task<bool> IsUsernameExistsAsync(string username);
        Task UpdateLastLoginAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Set IsActive = true/false вҖ” dГ№ng cho Activate/Deactivate.
        /// TГЎch riГӘng thay vГ¬ UpdateAsync Д‘б»ғ trГЎnh ghi Д‘ГЁ cГЎc field khГЎc.
        /// </summary>
        Task SetActiveAsync(int userId, bool isActive);

        /// <summary>
        /// Cбәӯp nhбәӯt chб»ү PasswordHash вҖ” tГЎch riГӘng vГ¬ UpdateAsync bбәЈo vб»Ү cб»ҷt nГ y.
        /// </summary>
        Task UpdatePasswordAsync(int userId, string newPasswordHash);

        /// <summary>
        /// TбәЎo user vГ  gГЎn Role trong 1 transaction вҖ” trГЎnh user khГҙng cГі Role.
        /// </summary>
        Task AddWithRoleAsync(User user, string roleName);

        /// <summary>
        /// Дҗб»•i role cho user: xГіa tбәҘt cбәЈ role cЕ©, gГЎn role mб»ӣi.
        /// DГ№ng transaction Д‘б»ғ Д‘бәЈm bбәЈo atomicity.
        /// </summary>
        Task ChangeRoleAsync(int userId, string newRoleName);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Authentication Service.
    /// Дҗб»Ӣnh nghД©a contract вҖ“ WinForms layer chб»ү biбәҝt Interface nГ y,
    /// khГҙng biбәҝt cГЎch implement bГӘn trong.
    /// </summary>
    public interface IAuthService
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// XГЎc thб»ұc username + password, trбәЈ vб»Ғ LoginResult.
        /// Form chб»ү gб»Қi 1 dГІng nГ y вҖ“ toГ n bб»ҷ logic nбәұm trong Service.
        /// </summary>
        Task<LoginResult> LoginAsync(string username, string password);

        /// <summary>
        /// Hash mбәӯt khбә©u bбәұng BCrypt (dГ№ng khi tбәЎo/Д‘б»•i mбәӯt khбә©u).
        /// </summary>
        string HashPassword(string plainPassword);

        /// <summary>
        /// XГЎc minh mбәӯt khбә©u nhбәӯp vГ o so vб»ӣi hash trong DB.
        /// </summary>
        bool VerifyPassword(string plainPassword, string hashedPassword);
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: IExpenseService.cs ---
========================================

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Service nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ quбәЈn lГҪ Chi phГӯ dб»ұ ГЎn (GДҗ8: UC-23 / GДҗ9: UC-Report-01).
    /// TбәҘt cбәЈ phЖ°ЖЎng thб»©c Д‘б»Ғu lГ  async Д‘б»ғ khГҙng chбә·n UI thread.
    /// </summary>
    public interface IExpenseService
    {
        // в”Җв”Җ Danh sГЎch в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy danh sГЎch chi phГӯ cб»§a mб»ҷt dб»ұ ГЎn (kГЁm CreatedBy).
        /// SбәҜp xбәҝp theo ExpenseDate giбәЈm dбә§n.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<Expense>> GetByProjectAsync(int projectId);

        // в”Җв”Җ CRUD в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// ThГӘm khoбәЈn chi phГӯ mб»ӣi.
        /// - Validation: Amount phбәЈi > 0; ExpenseDate khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc lб»ӣn hЖЎn ngГ y hiб»Үn tбәЎi.
        /// - Audit: CreatedById Д‘Ж°б»Јc gГЎn tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng tб»« AppSession.UserId.
        /// - CreatedAt Д‘Ж°б»Јc gГЎn tб»ұ Д‘б»ҷng DateTime.UtcNow.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddExpenseAsync(Expense expense);

        /// <summary>
        /// Cбәӯp nhбәӯt thГҙng tin khoбәЈn chi phГӯ Д‘ГЈ cГі.
        /// Validation tЖ°ЖЎng tб»ұ AddExpenseAsync (Amount > 0, ExpenseDate hб»Јp lб»Ү).
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateExpenseAsync(Expense expense);

        /// <summary>
        /// XГіa khoбәЈn chi phГӯ theo ID (hard delete).
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ lб»—i nбәҝu khГҙng tГ¬m thбәҘy bбәЈn ghi.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteExpenseAsync(int expenseId);

        // в”Җв”Җ Budget Summary в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ tГіm tбәҜt ngГўn sГЎch cб»§a mб»ҷt dб»ұ ГЎn:
        /// Budget (tб»« Project), TotalExpense (SUM tб»« Expense), Remaining, UsagePercent.
        /// TбәҘt cбәЈ tГӯnh toГЎn tiб»Ғn tб»Ү dГ№ng decimal вҖ“ KHГ”NG dГ№ng double/float.
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ null nбәҝu dб»ұ ГЎn khГҙng tб»“n tбәЎi.
        /// </summary>
        Task<ProjectBudgetSummaryDto?> GetProjectBudgetSummaryAsync(int projectId);

        // в”Җв”Җ BГЎo cГЎo (GДҗ9: UC-Report-01) в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy dб»Ҝ liб»Үu bГЎo cГЎo chi phГӯ vГ  ngГўn sГЎch dб»ұ ГЎn (ExpenseReportDto).
        ///
        /// Thiбәҝt kбәҝ:
        ///   - Khi projectId = null вҶ’ trбәЈ vб»Ғ tбәҘt cбәЈ dб»ұ ГЎn (bГЎo cГЎo tб»•ng hб»Јp).
        ///   - Khi projectId cГі giГЎ trб»Ӣ вҶ’ chб»ү trбәЈ vб»Ғ dб»Ҝ liб»Үu cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘Гі.
        ///   - Dб»Ҝ liб»Үu Д‘Ж°б»Јc "phбәіng hГіa" qua Projection .Select() tбәЎi Repository
        ///     вҶ’ khГҙng nбәЎp Entity rГЎc vГ o bб»ҷ nhб»ӣ.
        ///   - TrбәЈ vб»Ғ list rб»—ng nбәҝu khГҙng cГі dб»Ҝ liб»Үu (khГҙng throw exception).
        ///   - Mб»Қi trЖ°б»қng tiб»Ғn tб»Ү trong ExpenseReportDto Д‘б»Ғu lГ  decimal.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="projectId">
        ///   null = tбәҘt cбәЈ dб»ұ ГЎn;
        ///   cГі giГЎ trб»Ӣ = lб»Қc theo dб»ұ ГЎn cб»Ҙ thб»ғ.
        /// </param>
        Task<List<ExpenseReportDto>> GetExpenseReportDataAsync(int? projectId = null);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Service quбәЈn lГҪ dб»ұ ГЎn вҖ“ CRUD + thГ nh viГӘn + Д‘б»•i trбәЎng thГЎi.
    /// </summary>
    public interface IProjectService
    {
        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch dб»ұ ГЎn theo quyб»Ғn (Manager: tбәҘt cбәЈ, Developer: chб»ү dб»ұ ГЎn mГ¬nh).</summary>
        Task<List<Project>> GetProjectsForUserAsync(int userId, bool isManager);

        /// <summary>Chi tiбәҝt dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ (Members, Tasks, Expenses).</summary>
        Task<Project?> GetProjectDetailsAsync(int projectId);

        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateProjectAsync(Project project);
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProjectAsync(Project project);

        /// <summary>XГіa dб»ұ ГЎn вҖ“ chб»ү cho phГ©p khi chЖ°a cГі task.</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteProjectAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>Дҗб»•i trбәЎng thГЎi dб»ұ ГЎn (NotStarted/InProgress/OnHold/Completed/Cancelled).</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeStatusAsync(int projectId, string newStatus);

        // в”Җв”Җ QuбәЈn lГҪ thГ nh viГӘn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Danh sГЎch thГ nh viГӘn Д‘ang active cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn.</summary>
        Task<List<ProjectMember>> GetMembersAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>ThГӘm developer vГ o dб»ұ ГЎn vб»ӣi vai trГІ chб»ү Д‘б»Ӣnh.</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId, string projectRole);

        /// <summary>XГіa thГ nh viГӘn khб»Ҹi dб»ұ ГЎn (soft delete: set LeftAt).</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> RemoveMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Interface cho Task Service вҖ“ nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ quбәЈn lГҪ cГҙng viб»Үc GD4.
    ///
    /// GD4 bб»• sung so vб»ӣi GD1/GD3:
    ///   - CreateTaskAsync / UpdateTaskAsync: validate Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§
    ///   - UpdateProgressAsync: tб»ұ chuyб»ғn Status вҶ’ RESOLVED khi progress = 100
    ///   - UpdateStatusAsync: chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi workflow 10 bЖ°б»ӣc vб»ӣi validate
    ///   - GetLookupDataAsync: lбәҘy Priority, Status, Category cho dropdown frmTaskEdit
    ///   - GetTasksForReviewerAsync / GetTasksForTesterAsync: cho mГ n hГ¬nh Review/Test
    /// </summary>
    public interface ITaskService
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Sб»ұ kiб»Үn Д‘Ж°б»Јc kГӯch hoбәЎt khi cГі thay Д‘б»•i dб»Ҝ liб»Үu cГҙng viб»Үc.
        /// Sб»ӯ dб»Ҙng Д‘б»ғ Д‘б»“ng bб»ҷ UI (Refresh grid).
        /// </summary>
        event EventHandler TaskDataChanged;

        /// <summary>
        /// KГӯch hoбәЎt sб»ұ kiб»Үn TaskDataChanged thб»§ cГҙng tб»« bГӘn ngoГ i (e.g. tб»« ExpenseService).
        /// GiГәp Dashboard nhбәӯn biбәҝt cбә§n load lбәЎi dб»Ҝ liб»Үu.
        /// </summary>
        void NotifyDataChanged();

        // в”Җв”Җ Truy vбәҘn Д‘ЖЎn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Chi tiбәҝt task vб»ӣi Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§ navigation properties.
        /// DГ№ng cho frmTaskEdit вҖ” cбә§n Priority, Status, Category, Users, SubTasks.
        /// </summary>
        Task<TaskItem?> GetByIdAsync(int taskId);

        // в”Җв”Җ PhГўn trang + lб»Қc в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// PhГўn trang + lб»Қc kбәҝt hб»Јp вҖ” dГ№ng cho frmTaskList.
        /// TбәҘt cбәЈ tham sб»‘ nullable = tГ№y chб»Қn.
        /// TrбәЈ vб»Ғ (Items, TotalCount) Д‘б»ғ tГӯnh sб»‘ trang б»ҹ UI.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(List<TaskItem> Items, int TotalCount)> GetPagedAsync(
            int     page,
            int     pageSize,
            int?    projectId     = null,
            int?    assignedToId  = null,
            int?    statusId      = null,
            int?    priorityId    = null,
            int?    categoryId    = null,
            string? keyword       = null);

        // в”Җв”Җ Truy vбәҘn theo ngЖ°б»қi phб»Ҙ trГЎch в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Task chЖ°a hoГ n thГ nh Д‘Ж°б»Јc giao cho developer (mГ n hГ¬nh "CГҙng viб»Үc cб»§a tГҙi").
        /// Developer chб»ү thбәҘy task cб»§a chГӯnh mГ¬nh.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetMyTasksAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ review lбә§n 1 bб»ҹi reviewer.
        /// DГ№ng cho tab "Review" trong frmMyTasks hoбә·c frmTaskList.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer1Async(int reviewerId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ review lбә§n 2 bб»ҹi reviewer.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForReviewer2Async(int reviewerId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Task Д‘ang chб»қ test bб»ҹi tester.
        /// DГ№ng cho tab "Testing" trong frmMyTasks.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetTasksForTesterAsync(int testerId);

        // в”Җв”Җ CбәЈnh bГЎo / Dashboard в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>Task Д‘ГЈ quГЎ hбәЎn вҖ” widget cбәЈnh bГЎo Д‘б»Ҹ Dashboard.</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetOverdueTasksAsync();

        /// <summary>Task sбәҜp Д‘бәҝn hбәЎn trong N ngГ y вҖ” widget nhбәҜc nhб»ҹ vГ ng Dashboard.</summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetDueSoonTasksAsync(int days = 7);

        /// <summary>
        /// TГіm tбәҜt sб»‘ task theo Status trong 1 dб»ұ ГЎn.
        /// Kбәҝt quбәЈ: { "CREATED": 3, "IN-PROGRESS": 7, ... }
        /// DГ№ng cho pie chart Dashboard.
        Task<Dictionary<string, int>> GetStatusSummaryAsync(int projectId);

        /// <summary>
        /// Giai Д‘oбәЎn 6: TГӯnh toГЎn vГ  gom nhГіm cГЎc chб»ү sб»‘ / biб»ғu Д‘б»“ cho Dashboard.
        /// QuбәЈn lГҪ tб»•ng hб»Јp nбәҝu projectId = null (Admin), nбәҝu khГЎc null thГ¬ lб»Қc theo mб»ҷt dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘Гі.
        /// </summary>
        Task<DashboardStatsDto> GetDashboardStatsAsync(int? projectId = null);

        Task<List<BudgetReportDto>> GetBudgetReportAsync(int? projectId = null);
        Task<List<ProgressReportDto>> GetProgressReportAsync(int? projectId = null);

        // в”Җв”Җ CRUD в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// TбәЎo task mб»ӣi.
        /// Validate: Title khГҙng trб»‘ng, ProjectId > 0, PriorityId/StatusId/CategoryId hб»Јp lб»Ү.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateTaskAsync(TaskItem task);

        /// <summary>
        /// Cбәӯp nhбәӯt task.
        /// Validate: Title khГҙng trб»‘ng, task phбәЈi tб»“n tбәЎi.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateTaskAsync(TaskItem task);

        /// <summary>
        /// XГіa task.
        /// Validate: task khГҙng cГі sub-task (nбәҝu cГі thГ¬ khГҙng cho xГіa).
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteTaskAsync(int taskId);

        // в”Җв”Җ Cбәӯp nhбәӯt tiбәҝn Д‘б»ҷ & trбәЎng thГЎi в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// Cбәӯp nhбәӯt tiбәҝn Д‘б»ҷ % (0вҖ“100).
        ///   progress = 100 вҶ’ рҹҺү Task hoГ n thГ nh! IsCompleted = true, Status вҶ’ RESOLVED
        ///   progress &lt; 100 вҶ’ Cбәӯp nhбәӯt bГ¬nh thЖ°б»қng, IsCompleted = false
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProgressAsync(int taskId, byte progress);

        /// <summary>
        /// Chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi workflow vб»ӣi phГўn quyб»Ғn.
        ///   requesterId    вҖ” AppSession.UserId
        ///   requesterRoles вҖ” AppSession.Roles
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateStatusAsync(
            int taskId,
            int statusId,
            int requesterId,
            IList<string> requesterRoles);

        /// <summary>
        /// GГЎn reviewer/tester vГ  chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi trong 1 thao tГЎc.
        ///
        /// VГӯ dб»Ҙ: Developer xong вҶ’ gГЎn Reviewer1, chuyб»ғn sang REVIEW-1.
        ///   AssignAndTransitionAsync(taskId, reviewer1Id: 5, newStatus: "REVIEW-1")
        ///
        /// Validate: newStatus hб»Јp lб»Ү, userId gГЎn vГ o phбәЈi lГ  user active.
        /// </summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AssignAndTransitionAsync(
            int     taskId,
            string  newStatus,
            int?    reviewer1Id = null,
            int?    reviewer2Id = null,
            int?    testerId    = null);

        // в”Җв”Җ Lookup data cho dropdown в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Statuses (10 bЖ°б»ӣc), sбәҜp theo DisplayOrder.
        /// DГ№ng cho dropdown Status trong frmTaskEdit vГ  frmTaskList filter.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<Status>> GetAllStatusesAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Priorities (4 mб»©c), sбәҜp theo Level.
        /// DГ№ng cho dropdown Priority trong frmTaskEdit.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<Priority>> GetAllPrioritiesAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy tбәҘt cбәЈ Categories.
        /// DГ№ng cho dropdown Category trong frmTaskEdit.
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<Category>> GetAllCategoriesAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// LбәҘy toГ n bб»ҷ task cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘б»ғ hiб»ғn thб»Ӣ lГӘn Kanban Board.
        /// ДҗГЈ bao gб»“m logic sбәҜp xбәҝp: Priority (Critical -> Low) vГ  DueDate (Gбә§n -> Xa).
        /// </summary>
        Task<List<TaskItem>> GetBoardTasksAsync(int projectId);

        // в”Җв”Җ Giai Д‘oбәЎn 7: Comment & Attachment в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
        
        Task<List<Comment>> GetCommentsAsync(int taskId);
        
        Task<(bool Success, string Message, Comment? Data)> AddCommentAsync(
            int taskId, 
            string content, 
            int requesterId, 
            IList<string> requesterRoles);

        Task<List<Attachment>> GetAttachmentsAsync(int taskId);
        
        Task<(bool Success, string Message, Attachment? Data)> UploadAttachmentAsync(
            int taskId, 
            string sourcePath, 
            int requesterId, 
            IList<string> requesterRoles);

        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteAttachmentAsync(
            int attachmentId, 
            int requesterId, 
            IList<string> requesterRoles);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services
{
    public interface IUserService
    {
        /// <summary>LбәҘy TбәӨT Cбәў user (active + inactive) kГЁm Roles вҖ” dГ№ng cho mГ n hГ¬nh Admin.</summary>
        Task<List<User>> GetAllUsersAsync();

        /// <summary>LбәҘy user Д‘ang active вҖ” dГ№ng cho dropdown, assign task.</summary>
        Task<List<User>> GetAllActiveUsersAsync();

        Task<User?> GetByIdAsync(int id);

        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateUserAsync(
            string username, string fullName, string email,
            string password, string roleName, string? phone = null);

        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateUserAsync(User user);

        /// <summary>Soft delete вҖ“ set IsActive = false.</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeactivateUserAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>KГӯch hoбәЎt lбәЎi вҖ“ set IsActive = true (ngЖ°б»Јc cб»§a Deactivate).</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ActivateUserAsync(int userId);

        /// <summary>Дҗб»•i mбәӯt khбә©u вҖ“ verify old pass trЖ°б»ӣc khi hash new pass.</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangePasswordAsync(
            int userId, string oldPassword, string newPassword);

        /// <summary>Дҗб»•i vai trГІ user вҖ“ chб»ү Admin mб»ӣi Д‘Ж°б»Јc gб»Қi. XГіa role cЕ©, gГЎn role mб»ӣi.</summary>
        Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeRoleAsync(int userId, string newRoleName);
    }
}

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Helpers;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triб»ғn khai IAuthService вҖ“ xГЎc thб»ұc ngЖ°б»қi dГ№ng (Login).
    ///
    /// Luб»“ng Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp:
    ///   1. Validate username/password khГҙng rб»—ng
    ///   2. TГ¬m user trong DB (chб»ү user active)
    ///   3. Verify BCrypt password qua PasswordHelper
    ///   4. Load danh sГЎch Roles Д‘б»ғ phГўn quyб»Ғn
    ///   5. Map User вҶ’ UserSessionDto (khГҙng expose PasswordHash)
    ///   6. UpdateLastLogin (Async/Await Synchronized)
    ///   7. TrбәЈ LoginResult.Ok hoбә·c LoginResult.Fail
    ///
    /// DГ№ng Result Pattern (LoginResult) thay vГ¬ throw Exception
    /// cho lб»—i nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ вҶ’ Form xб»ӯ lГҪ gб»Қn hЖЎn, khГҙng cбә§n try-catch.
    /// </summary>
    public class AuthService : IAuthService
    {
        private readonly IUserRepository _userRepo;

        // Inject IUserRepository qua constructor (DI Container cung cбәҘp)
        public AuthService(IUserRepository userRepo) => _userRepo = userRepo;

        public async Task<LoginResult> LoginAsync(string username, string password)
        {
            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 1: Validate Д‘бә§u vГ o (guard clauses) ---
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(username))
                return LoginResult.Fail("вҡ  Vui lГІng nhбәӯp tГӘn Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp.");

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(password))
                return LoginResult.Fail("вҡ  Vui lГІng nhбәӯp mбәӯt khбә©u.");

            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 2: TГ¬m user trong DB ---
            // GetByUsernameAsync chб»ү trбәЈ user cГі IsActive = true
            var user = await _userRepo.GetByUsernameAsync(username.Trim());

            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 3: Verify BCrypt password ---
            // DГ№ng thГҙng bГЎo chung cho cбәЈ 2 trЖ°б»қng hб»Јp sai username / sai password
            // вҶ’ trГЎnh tiбәҝt lб»ҷ username cГі tб»“n tбәЎi trong hб»Ү thб»‘ng khГҙng (security)
            if (user == null || !PasswordHelper.Verify(password, user.PasswordHash))
                return LoginResult.Fail("вҡ  TГӘn Д‘Дғng nhбәӯp hoбә·c mбәӯt khбә©u khГҙng Д‘Гәng.");

            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 4: Load Roles Д‘б»ғ phГўn quyб»Ғn (eager load) ---
            var userWithRoles = await _userRepo.GetWithRolesAsync(user.Id);
            if (userWithRoles == null)
                return LoginResult.Fail("вҡ  KhГҙng thб»ғ tбәЈi thГҙng tin quyб»Ғn. Vui lГІng thб»ӯ lбәЎi.");

            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 5: Map вҶ’ DTO (khГҙng trбәЈ User entity thГҙ ra ngoГ i Service) ---
            var dto = UserSessionMapper.ToDto(userWithRoles);

            // --- BЖ°б»ӣc 6: Cбәӯp nhбәӯt LastLogin (Async/Await Synchronized) ---
            await _userRepo.UpdateLastLoginAsync(user.Id);

            return LoginResult.Ok(dto);
        }

        // Delegate sang PasswordHelper вҖ“ AuthService khГҙng chб»©a BCrypt logic trб»ұc tiбәҝp
        // NguyГӘn tбәҜc Single Responsibility: AuthService lo flow, PasswordHelper lo thuбәӯt toГЎn
        public string HashPassword(string plainPassword) => PasswordHelper.Hash(plainPassword);
        public bool VerifyPassword(string plain, string hashed) => PasswordHelper.Verify(plain, hashed);
    }
}


========================================
--- FILE: UserSessionMapper.cs ---
========================================

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Auth
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Chuyб»ғn Д‘б»•i User entity вҶ’ UserSessionDto.
    ///
    /// TГЎch ra file riГӘng vГ¬:
    ///   - AuthService khГҙng nГӘn chб»©a mapping logic (Single Responsibility)
    ///   - Dб»… tГЎi dГ№ng khi cбә§n refresh session sau nГ y
    ///   - Dб»… unit test mapping Д‘б»ҷc lбәӯp vб»ӣi logic login
    ///
    /// UserSessionDto chб»ү chб»©a thГҙng tin cбә§n thiбәҝt cho UI,
    /// Д‘бә·c biб»Үt KHГ”NG cГі PasswordHash вҶ’ an toГ n hЖЎn khi lЖ°u vГ o AppSession.
    /// </summary>
    internal static class UserSessionMapper
    {
        internal static UserSessionDto ToDto(User user) => new()
        {
            Id         = user.Id,
            Username   = user.Username,
            FullName   = user.FullName,
            Email      = user.Email,
            AvatarPath = user.AvatarPath,
            // LбәҘy tГӘn cГЎc Role tб»« navigation property UserRoles вҶ’ Role
            // VГӯ dб»Ҙ kбәҝt quбәЈ: ["Admin"] hoбә·c ["Manager"] hoбә·c ["Developer"]
            Roles      = user.UserRoles?
                .Select(ur => ur.Role.Name)
                .ToList()
                ?? new List<string>()
        };
    }
}

--- FILE: ExpenseService.cs ---

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.DTOs;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Expenses
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Triб»ғn khai nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ QuбәЈn lГҪ Chi phГӯ (GДҗ8: UC-23 / GДҗ9: UC-Report-01).
    /// TuГўn thб»§ quy tбәҜc Financial Precision vГ  Audit Trail.
    /// </summary>
    public class ExpenseService : IExpenseService
    {
        private readonly IExpenseRepository _expenseRepo;
        private readonly IProjectRepository _projectRepo;
        private readonly ITaskService _taskService;

        public ExpenseService(IExpenseRepository expenseRepo, IProjectRepository projectRepo, ITaskService taskService)
        {
            _expenseRepo = expenseRepo;
            _projectRepo = projectRepo;
            _taskService = taskService;
        }

        public async Task<List<Expense>> GetByProjectAsync(int projectId)
        {
            return await _expenseRepo.GetByProjectAsync(projectId);
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddExpenseAsync(Expense expense)
        {
            // 1. Validation
            if (expense.Amount <= 0)
                return (false, "Sб»‘ tiб»Ғn phбәЈi lб»ӣn hЖЎn 0.");

            if (expense.ExpenseDate > DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today))
                return (false, "NgГ y chi phГӯ khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc vЖ°б»Јt quГЎ ngГ y hiб»Үn tбәЎi.");

            if (expense.ProjectId <= 0)
                return (false, "Vui lГІng chб»Қn dб»ұ ГЎn hб»Јp lб»Ү.");

            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(expense.ExpenseType))
                return (false, "Vui lГІng chб»Қn loбәЎi chi phГӯ.");

            try
            {
                // Audit Trail: Thб»қi Д‘iб»ғm phГЎt sinh
                expense.CreatedAt = DateTime.UtcNow;

                await _expenseRepo.AddAsync(expense);
                _taskService.NotifyDataChanged(); // Дҗб»“ng bб»ҷ Dashboard
                return (true, "ThГӘm chi phГӯ thГ nh cГҙng.");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, $"Lб»—i server: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateExpenseAsync(Expense expense)
        {
            if (expense.Amount <= 0)
                return (false, "Sб»‘ tiб»Ғn phбәЈi lб»ӣn hЖЎn 0.");

            if (expense.ExpenseDate > DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today))
                return (false, "NgГ y chi phГӯ khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc vЖ°б»Јt quГЎ ngГ y hiб»Үn tбәЎi.");

            try
            {
                var existing = await _expenseRepo.GetByIdAsync(expense.Id);
                if (existing == null) return (false, "KhГҙng tГ¬m thбәҘy khoбәЈn chi phГӯ nГ y.");

                // Cбәӯp nhбәӯt cГЎc trЖ°б»қng cho phГ©p
                existing.ProjectId   = expense.ProjectId;
                existing.ExpenseType = expense.ExpenseType;
                existing.Amount      = expense.Amount;
                existing.ExpenseDate = expense.ExpenseDate;
                existing.Note        = expense.Note;

                await _expenseRepo.UpdateAsync(existing);
                _taskService.NotifyDataChanged();
                return (true, "Cбәӯp nhбәӯt chi phГӯ thГ nh cГҙng.");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, $"Lб»—i server: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteExpenseAsync(int expenseId)
        {
            try
            {
                var existing = await _expenseRepo.GetByIdAsync(expenseId);
                if (existing == null) return (false, "KhГҙng tГ¬m thбәҘy khoбәЈn chi phГӯ nГ y.");

                await _expenseRepo.DeleteAsync(expenseId);
                _taskService.NotifyDataChanged();
                return (true, "XГіa chi phГӯ thГ nh cГҙng.");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                return (false, $"Lб»—i server: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }

        public async Task<ProjectBudgetSummaryDto?> GetProjectBudgetSummaryAsync(int projectId)
        {
            var project = await _projectRepo.GetByIdAsync(projectId);
            if (project == null) return null;

            var totalExpense = await _expenseRepo.GetTotalByProjectAsync(projectId);

            return new ProjectBudgetSummaryDto
            {
                ProjectId    = project.Id,
                ProjectName  = project.Name,
                Budget       = project.Budget,
                TotalExpense = totalExpense
            };
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// GДҗ9 вҖ“ UC-Report-01: LбәҘy dб»Ҝ liб»Үu bГЎo cГЎo chi phГӯ vГ  ngГўn sГЎch.
        ///
        /// Service chб»ү lГ m nhiб»Үm vб»Ҙ Д‘iб»Ғu phб»‘i (orchestration):
        ///   - б»Ұy thГЎc toГ n bб»ҷ truy vбәҘn xuб»‘ng Repository (tuГўn thб»§ SRP).
        ///   - Repository chб»Ӣu trГЎch nhiб»Үm Projection, AsNoTracking, GroupBy.
        ///   - Service bбәҜt exception vГ  bб»Қc lбәЎi thГ nh list rб»—ng thay vГ¬ Д‘б»ғ UI crash.
        /// </summary>
        public async Task<List<ExpenseReportDto>> GetExpenseReportDataAsync(int? projectId = null)
        {
            return await _expenseRepo.GetExpenseReportDataAsync(projectId);
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: ProjectService.cs ---

using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Entities;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces;
using TaskFlowManagement.Core.Interfaces.Services;

namespace TaskFlowManagement.Core.Services.Projects
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Nghiб»Үp vб»Ҙ quбәЈn lГҪ dб»ұ ГЎn: tбәЎo/sб»ӯa/xГіa dб»ұ ГЎn, Д‘б»•i trбәЎng thГЎi, quбәЈn lГҪ thГ nh viГӘn.
    /// </summary>
    public class ProjectService : IProjectService
    {
        private readonly IProjectRepository _projectRepo;

        public ProjectService(IProjectRepository projectRepo)
            => _projectRepo = projectRepo;

        // Danh sГЎch dб»ұ ГЎn theo quyб»Ғn
        public Task<List<Project>> GetProjectsForUserAsync(int userId, bool isManager)
            => isManager ? _projectRepo.GetAllAsync() : _projectRepo.GetByMemberAsync(userId);

        // Chi tiбәҝt Д‘бә§y Д‘б»§
        public Task<Project?> GetProjectDetailsAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetWithDetailsAsync(projectId);

        // TбәЎo dб»ұ ГЎn mб»ӣi
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> CreateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TГӘn dб»ұ ГЎn khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc Д‘б»ғ trб»‘ng.");

            await _projectRepo.AddAsync(project);
            return (true, $"Dб»ұ ГЎn \"{project.Name}\" Д‘ГЈ Д‘Ж°б»Јc tбәЎo thГ nh cГҙng.");
        }

        // Cбәӯp nhбәӯt dб»ұ ГЎn
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> UpdateProjectAsync(Project project)
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(project.Name))
                return (false, "TГӘn dб»ұ ГЎn khГҙng Д‘Ж°б»Јc Д‘б»ғ trб»‘ng.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateAsync(project);
            return (true, "Cбәӯp nhбәӯt dб»ұ ГЎn thГ nh cГҙng.");
        }

        // XГіa dб»ұ ГЎn вҖ“ kiб»ғm tra cГі task chЖ°a
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> DeleteProjectAsync(int projectId)
        {
            if (await _projectRepo.HasTasksAsync(projectId))
                return (false, "KhГҙng thб»ғ xГіa dб»ұ ГЎn Д‘ГЈ cГі cГҙng viб»Үc. HГЈy xГіa cГҙng viб»Үc trЖ°б»ӣc hoбә·c chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi Cancelled.");

            await _projectRepo.DeleteAsync(projectId);
            return (true, "XГіa dб»ұ ГЎn thГ nh cГҙng.");
        }

        // Дҗб»•i trбәЎng thГЎi dб»ұ ГЎn
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> ChangeStatusAsync(int projectId, string newStatus)
        {
            var validStatuses = new[] { "NotStarted", "InProgress", "OnHold", "Completed", "Cancelled" };
            if (!validStatuses.Contains(newStatus))
                return (false, $"TrбәЎng thГЎi \"{newStatus}\" khГҙng hб»Јp lб»Ү.");

            await _projectRepo.UpdateStatusAsync(projectId, newStatus);
            return (true, $"ДҗГЈ chuyб»ғn trбәЎng thГЎi thГ nh {newStatus}.");
        }

        // в”Җв”Җ QuбәЈn lГҪ thГ nh viГӘn в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

        public Task<List<ProjectMember>> GetMembersAsync(int projectId)
            => _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);

        // ThГӘm thГ nh viГӘn вҖ“ kiб»ғm tra trГ№ng
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> AddMemberAsync(
            int projectId, int userId, string projectRole)
        {
            // Kiб»ғm tra Д‘ГЈ lГ  thГ nh viГӘn chЖ°a
            var members = await _projectRepo.GetMembersAsync(projectId);
            if (members.Any(m => m.UserId == userId))
                return (false, "NgЖ°б»қi dГ№ng Д‘ГЈ lГ  thГ nh viГӘn cб»§a dб»ұ ГЎn nГ y.");

            var member = new ProjectMember
            {
                ProjectId   = projectId,
                UserId      = userId,
                ProjectRole = projectRole,
                JoinedAt    = DateTime.UtcNow
            };
            await _projectRepo.AddMemberAsync(member);
            return (true, "ThГӘm thГ nh viГӘn thГ nh cГҙng.");
        }

        // XГіa thГ nh viГӘn (soft delete: set LeftAt)
        public async Task<(bool Success, string Message)> RemoveMemberAsync(int projectId, int userId)
        {
            await _projectRepo.RemoveMemberAsync(projectId, userId);
            return (true, "ДҗГЈ xГіa thГ nh viГӘn khб»Ҹi dб»ұ ГЎn.");
        }
    }
}

--- FILE: TaskService.cs ---
